there is actually a trick to duplicate copper, if you turn copper into slabs by using a stone cutter, for some reason it becomes 8 slabs instead of 2. Therefore, you can just quadruple copper into slabs. After doing so, just stack the slabs on top of each other to make them 1 block and repeat the process! Way faster than mining it all.
